<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Filip-Lars Topolak" aria-label="Filip-Lars Topolak" role="img">FT</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>(at) full throttle</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136">Filip-Lars Topolak</a> - Friday, 19 December 2025, 10:38 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/(æt) fʊl ˈθrɒtəl/</p>
<p><strong>moving or progressing as fast as possible:</strong></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>She was roaring up the freeway <strong>at full throttle</strong>.</em></span></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em><strong>S polnim plinom</strong> je drvela po avtocesti.</em></span></p>
<p>From: (<a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/at-full-throttle">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/at-full-throttle</a><span style="font-size:1rem;">)</span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: (at) full throttle" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91183"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: (at) full throttle" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: (at) full throttle"></i></a><a class='icon' title="Delete" href="deleteentry.php?id=579823&amp;mode=delete&amp;entry=91183&amp;prevmode=letter&amp;hook=ALL"><i class="icon fa fa-trash-can fa-fw "  title="Delete entry: (at) full throttle" role="img" aria-label="Delete entry: (at) full throttle"></i></a><a class='icon' title="Edit" href="edit.php?cmid=579823&amp;id=91183&amp;mode=letter&amp;hook=ALL"><i class="icon fa fa-pen fa-fw "  title="Edit entry: (at) full throttle" role="img" aria-label="Edit entry: (at) full throttle"></i></a><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/portfolio/add.php?ca_id=579823&ca_entryid=91183&sesskey=h7vqXICERO&callbackcomponent=mod_glossary&callbackclass=glossary_entry_portfolio_caller&course=12136&callerformats=plainhtml%2Cleap2a&instance=1" id="action_link6954ff5fa85a611" class="action-icon mx-1 p-1 btn btn-link icon-no-margin"  title="Export to portfolio"  aria-label="Export to portfolio" ><i class="icon fa fa-plus fa-fw portfolio-add-icon smallicon" aria-hidden="true" ></i></a></span><div><div style="display:none" id="cmt-tmpl"><div class="comment-message"><div class="comment-message-meta me-3"><span class="picture">___picture___</span><span class="user">___name___</span> - <div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>A</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Katarina Dimitrijević" aria-label="Katarina Dimitrijević" role="img">KD</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Absence makes the heart grow fonder</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136">Katarina Dimitrijević</a> - Sunday, 9 November 2025, 11:46 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>Idiom</p>
<p>/ˈæbsəns meɪks ðə hɑːt ɡrəʊ ˈfɒndə/</p>
<p><strong>When people we love are not with us, we love them even more.</strong></p>
<p>E.g. <span style="color:#7d9fd3;">A<em>s far as my own experience goes, this is a case in which <strong>absence makes the heart grow fonder</strong>.</em></span></p>
<p>Slovenian translation: <span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>Po mojih izkušnjah je to primer, ko odsotnost povzroči, da nekoga še bolj pogrešaš. </em></span></p>
<p>From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/us/dictionary/english/absence-makes-the-heart-grow-fonder">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/us/dictionary/english/absence-makes-the-heart-grow-fonder</a></p></div></td></tr><tr <p>/ˈæɡ.rə.veɪt/</p>
<p><strong>to make a disease worse:</strong></p>
<p><em>The treatment only aggravated the condition.</em></p>
<p><em>Terapija je le poslabšala stanje. </em></p>

<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˈeɪ.li.ə.neɪt</span>/</p>
<p><strong>to make someone feel that they are different and not part of a group:</strong></p>
<p>Example: Disagreements can alienate teenagers from their families.</p>
<p>Translation: Nesporazumi lahko odtujijo najstnike od <span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><s>svojih</s></span> <strong><span style="color:#da261b;">njihovih</span></strong> družin.</p>

<p> /əˈmiːl.jə.reɪt/</p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">/</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">æt iːʧ ˈʌðəz θrəʊts</span><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">/</span></p>

<p><strong>an official examination of the accounts of a business: </strong></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>An internal <strong>audit</strong> uncovered £11.5 million in payments to dead beneficiaries.</em></span></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>Notranja <strong>revizija</strong> je razkrila 11,5 milijona funtov izplačil umrlim upravičencem.</em></span></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Maj Rengeo" aria-label="Maj Rengeo" role="img">MR</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>average Joe</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136">Maj Rengeo</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 3:28 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">noun, idiom</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">/</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:11.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Helvetica, sans-serif;color:#373737;background:#FFFFFF;" xml:lang="en-si"> </span><span lang="en-si" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ˈævᵊrɪʤ ʤəʊ/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">an ordinary, typical person.</span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">He says it takes him longer than the average Joe to get ready for work.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">Pravi, da se za delo pripravlja dlje kot kot povprečen človek.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/us/dictionary/english/average-joe">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/us/dictionary/english/average-joe</a></span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: average Joe" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90821"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: average Joe" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: average Joe"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90821&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5fca07c" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5fca07c" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5fca07c">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5fca07c" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5fca07c" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5fca07c" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5fca07c" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5fca07c" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5fca07c"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5fca07c" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>B</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53398&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Luka Segečić" aria-label="Luka Segečić" role="img">LS</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>bait &amp; switch</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53398&amp;course=12136">Luka Segečić</a> - Monday, 17 November 2025, 2:56 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/beɪt/ /ænd/ /swɪʧ/</p>
<p>a method of selling in which a product is advertised at a very low price to attract customers, who are then persuaded to buy a different product at a higher price</p>
<p>E.g. <em>It seems to him that many brokers have been doing a bait-and-switch, luring customers with low rates and fees, then increasing those costs near the closing date.</em></p>
<p><em>Zdi se mu, da so mnogi posredniki uporabljali strategijo »vaba in zamenjava«, privabljali stranke z nizkimi obrestmi in provizijami, nato pa so te stroške proti datumu zaključka posla zvišali.</em></p>
<p>from: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/bait-and-switch</p>
<p>Luka Segečić </p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: bait &amp;amp; switch" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90762"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: bait &amp;amp; switch" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: bait &amp;amp; switch"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90762&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5fcbf70" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5fcbf70" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5fcbf70">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5fcbf70" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5fcbf70" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5fcbf70" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5fcbf70" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5fcbf70" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5fcbf70"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5fcbf70" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>
 </td></tr></table>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Nena Horvat" aria-label="Nena Horvat" role="img">NH</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Be subject to something</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136">Nena Horvat</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 1:54 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p><span style="font-size:1rem;">Phrase</span></p>
<p>/biː ˈsʌb.dʒekt tə ˈsʌm.θɪŋ/</p>
<p>To have or <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/experience">experience</a> a <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/particular">particular</a> thing, <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/especially">especially</a> something <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/unpleasant">unpleasant</a>.</p>
<p>In <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/recent">recent</a> <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/year">years</a>, she has been <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/subject">subject</a> to <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/attack">attacks</a> of <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/depression">depression</a>.</p>
<p>V zadnjih letih je bila podvržena napadom depresije.</p>
<p>Source: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/be-subject-to?q=be+subject+to+something">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/be-subject-to?q=be+subject+to+something</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Be subject to something" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90883"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Be subject to something" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Be subject to something"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90883&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5fcd607" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5fcd607" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5fcd607">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5fcd607" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5fcd607" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5fcd607" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5fcd607" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5fcd607" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5fcd607"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5fcd607" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=47211&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Sara Lesjak" aria-label="Sara Lesjak" role="img">SL</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Before you can say Jack Robinson</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=47211&amp;course=12136">Sara Lesjak</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 9:28 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span class="pos">idiom</span><span class="di-info"> <span class="ddivide"> </span><span class="lml--5"> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="frnorm">/bɪˈfɔː</span> <span class="frnorm"><span>jʊ</span></span> <span>kən</span> <span>seɪ</span> <span>ʤæk</span> <span class="frnorm"><span>ˈrɒbɪnsᵊn</span>/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">used to say that something happens very quickly:</p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="eg">example: Before you could say Jack Robinson, she'd jumped into the car and driven away.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Translation: Skočila je v avto in se odpeljala, preden bi lahko opazil.</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/before-you-can-say-jack-robinson">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/before-you-can-say-jack-robinson</a></p></div></td></tr><tr <p><span class="daud"> </span><span class="pron dpron">/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">bɪˈɡet</span>/</span></p>
<p><span class="pron dpron">to cause</span></p>
<p><span class="pron dpron">Poverty begets hunger, and hunger begets crime.</span></p>
<div class="ddef_h"> </div>
<div class="def-body ddef_b">
<div class="examp dexamp">Revščina povzroča lakoto, lakota pa kriminal.</div>

style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;color:rgb(0,0,0);"><span class="s1" style="font-family:UICTFontTextStyleBody;font-size:18.25px;">From: </span><a <table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=54239&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Valentina Mavrič" aria-label="Valentina Mavrič" role="img">VM</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Bob's your uncle</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=54239&amp;course=12136">Valentina Mavrič</a> - Monday, 15 December 2025, 6:38 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p><span class="fr_norm">/bɒbz</span> <span class="fr_norm">jɔːr</span> <span class="fr_norm">ˈʌŋkᵊl/</span></p>
<p><span class="fr_norm">used to mean that something will happen very quickly and simply</span></p>
<p><span class="fr_norm">Just tell them you're a friend of mine and, Bob's your uncle, you'll get the job.</span></p>
<p><span class="fr_norm">Samo povej jim, da si moj prijatelj, in to je to – služba je tvoja.</span></p>
<p><span class="fr_norm">source: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/bob?q=Bob%27s+your+uncle</span></p>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>C</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Brina Mohar" aria-label="Brina Mohar" role="img">BM</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>cajole</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136">Brina Mohar</a> - Sunday, 14 December 2025, 9:44 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>verb</p>
<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">kəˈdʒəʊl</span>/</p>
<p>to persuade someone to do something they might not want to do, by pleasant talk and promises, sometimes ones which are false</p>
<p>I managed to cajole her out of leaving too early.</p>
<p>Uspela sem jo pregovoriti, da ni prezgodaj odšla.</p>
<p>From: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/cajole </p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: cajole" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90865"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: cajole" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: cajole"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90865&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5fd578e" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5fd578e" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5fd578e">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">1</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5fd578e" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5fd578e" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5fd578e" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5fd578e" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5fd578e" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5fd578e"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5fd578e" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Filip-Lars Topolak" aria-label="Filip-Lars Topolak" role="img">FT</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>calibre</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136">Filip-Lars Topolak</a> - Sunday, 16 November 2025, 5:12 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun</p>
<p>(US caliber)</p>
<p>UK /ˈkæl.ɪ.bər/ <br />US /ˈkæl.ə.bɚ/</p>
<p><strong>the quality of someone or something, especially someone's ability:</strong></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>If teaching paid more it might attract people of (a) higher <strong>calibre</strong>.</em></span></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>Če bi bilo poučevanje bolje plačano, bi lahko privabilo ljudi višjega <strong>kova</strong>.</em></span></p>
<p>From: (<a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/calibre">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/calibre</a>)</p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td <table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Maj Rengeo" aria-label="Maj Rengeo" role="img">MR</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Calumny</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136">Maj Rengeo</a> - Friday, 19 December 2025, 7:29 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">noun (formal)</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">/</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ˈ</span><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">k</span><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">æ</span><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">l.əm.ni/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">(the act of making) a statement about someone that is not true and is intended to damage the reputation of that person.</span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">He was subjected to the most vicious calumny, but he never complained and never sued.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">Bil je podvržen najgroznejšim klevetam, vendar se ni nikoli pritoževal in nikoli tožil.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">From: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/us/dictionary/english/calumny</p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Calumny" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90772"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Calumny" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Calumny"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90772&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5fd80e4" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5fd80e4" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5fd80e4">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5fd80e4" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5fd80e4" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5fd80e4" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5fd80e4" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5fd80e4" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5fd80e4"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5fd80e4" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=54239&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Valentina Mavrič" aria-label="Valentina Mavrič" role="img">VM</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>carry/take coals to Newcastle</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=54239&amp;course=12136">Valentina Mavrič</a> - Sunday, 9 November 2025, 11:47 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/kæri/teɪk kəʊlz tə ˈnjuːkɑːsl/</p>
<p>to supply something to a place or person that already has a lot of that particular thing</p>
<p>Exporting pine to Scandinavia seems like carrying coals to Newcastle.</p>
<p>Izvoz borov v Skandinavijo se zdi kot nošenje vode v Savo.</p>
<p>Source: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/carry-take-coals-to-newcastle?q=carry%2Ftake+coals+to+Newcastle</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Katarina Dimitrijević" aria-label="Katarina Dimitrijević" role="img">KD</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Chinese whispers</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136">Katarina Dimitrijević</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 3:26 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/tʃaɪˈniːz ˈwɪspəz/</p>
<p><span class="mw_t_bc">A</span><strong class="mw_t_bc"> </strong>situation in which a piece of information is passed from one person to the next and is changed slightly each time it is told.</p>
<p>e.g. Unplanned pregnancies, infidelities, theft, drug feuds (money owed, territories infringed upon), <span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><strong><em>Chinese whispers</em></strong></span>, blatant lies, betrayal, violence, crime, shady exchanges, and the list goes on.</p>
<p>Translation: Nepričakovane nosečnosti, nezvestobe, kraje, spori zaradi drog (dolgovani denar, kršenje <span style="color:#da261b;">teritorialnih meja</span>), <em><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><strong>gluhi telefoni</strong></span></em>, očitne laži, izdaja, nasilje, zločin, sumljivi posli – in seznam se kar nadaljuje.</p>
<p>From: <a href="https://www.merriam-webster.com/dictionary/Chinese%20whispers">https://www.merriam-webster.com/dictionary/Chinese%20whispers</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Chinese whispers" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90666"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Chinese whispers" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Chinese whispers"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90666&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5fda4aa" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5fda4aa" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5fda4aa">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5fda4aa" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5fda4aa" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5fda4aa" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5fda4aa" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5fda4aa" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5fda4aa"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5fda4aa" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<p class="p1" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;color:#000000;"><span class="s2" style="font-family:UICTFontTextStyleEmphasizedBody;font-weight:bold;font-size:18.25px;"> </span></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50997&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Miha Kolenc" aria-label="Miha Kolenc" role="img">MK</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>compulsion</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50997&amp;course=12136">Miha Kolenc</a> - Monday, 15 December 2025, 9:08 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun</p>
<p> <span class="pron dpron">/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">kəmˈpʌl.ʃ<span class="sp dsp">ə</span>n</span>/</span></p>
<p class="p1"><strong>a very strong feeling of wanting to do something repeatedly that is difficult to control</strong></p>
<p class="p1">Example: Management felt no compulsion to provide housing for families.</p>
<p class="p1">Translation: Uprava se ni čutila dolžne, da bi družinam priskrbela stanovanja.</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=47211&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Sara Lesjak" aria-label="Sara Lesjak" role="img">SL</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>contention</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=47211&amp;course=12136">Sara Lesjak</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 9:19 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span class="pos">noun</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="pron">/</span><span class="ipa">kənˈten.ʃ</span><span class="sp">ə</span><span class="ipa">n</span><span class="pron">/</span> </p>
<p class="MsoNormal">The disagreement that results from opposing arguments:</p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="eg">example: There's a lot of contention about that </span>issue<span class="eg"> - for every </span>person<span class="eg"> </span>firmly<span class="eg"> in favour, there's someone </span>fiercely<span class="eg"> against it<i>.</i></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="eg">Translation: Glede te teme je veliko sporov - za vsako osebo, ki je močno za, obstaja nekdo, ki je izrecno proti. </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="eg">From: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/contention</span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: contention" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91246"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: contention" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: contention"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91246&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5fdf3df" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5fdf3df" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5fdf3df">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5fdf3df" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5fdf3df" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5fdf3df" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5fdf3df" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5fdf3df" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5fdf3df"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5fdf3df" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Manca Panjan" aria-label="Manca Panjan" role="img">MP</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>contentious</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136">Manca Panjan</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 10:37 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adjective</p>
<p>/kənˈtenʃəs/</p>
<p><strong>Likely to cause people to disagree</strong></p>
<p>Example sentence: Both views are highly contentious.</p>
<p>Translation: Obe stališči sta zelo sporni.</p>
<p>Source: <a href="https://www.oxfordlearnersdictionaries.com/definition/english/contentious?q=contentious">contentious adjective - Definition, pictures, pronunciation and usage notes | Oxford Advanced Learner's Dictionary at OxfordLearnersDictionaries.com</a> </p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Špela Švab" aria-label="Špela Švab" role="img">ŠŠ</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>contrived</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136">Špela Švab</a> - Thursday, 20 November 2025, 2:11 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adjective</p>
<p>/kənˈtraɪvd/</p>
<p><strong>Artificial and difficult to believe.</strong></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">American dictionary: <strong>Too <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/obviously">obviously</a> <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/design">designed</a> to <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/produce">produce</a> a <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/particular">particular</a> <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/result">result</a>, and <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/therefore">therefore</a> not <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/seeming">seeming</a> to <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/happen">happen</a> <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/naturally">naturally.</a></strong></span></p>
<p>I<span style="color:#000000;"> <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/enjoy">enjoyed</a> the <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/film">film</a>, but <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/felt">felt</a> the <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/ending">ending</a> was a <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/bit">bit</a> contrived.</span></p>
<p>Film mi je bil všeč, a konec se mi je zdel nekoliko prisiljen oziroma umeten.</p>
<p>Source:<a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/contrived">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/contrived</a></p>

<p>/kɒzˈmɒɡənɪ/</p>
<p>the study of the origin and development of the universe or of a particular system in the universe, such as the solar system</p>
<p>While myth is fiction posing as history and cosmogony, its function is to connect humans with the divine.</p>
<p>Čeprav je mit fikcija, ki se izdaja za zgodovino in kozmogonijo, je njegova funkcija povezati ljudi z božanskim.</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Nena Horvat" aria-label="Nena Horvat" role="img">NH</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Covenant</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136">Nena Horvat</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 1:53 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p><span style="font-size:1rem;">Noun</span></p>

<p>(Law) A <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/formal">formal</a> <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/agreement">agreement</a> or <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/promise">promise</a> between two or more <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/people">people</a>.</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50197&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Petja Božič" aria-label="Petja Božič" role="img">PB</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Culture shock</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50197&amp;course=12136">Petja Božič</a> - Sunday, 21 December 2025, 10:11 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><div class="pos-header dpos-h">
<div class="di-title"><span class="hw dhw">culture shock</span></div>
<div class="posgram dpos-g hdib lmr-5"><span class="pos dpos" title="A word that refers to a person, place, idea, event or thing.">noun</span> <span class="gram dgram"><a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/help/codes.html"> </a></span></div>
<span class="uk dpron-i"><span class="daud"> </span><span class="pron dpron">/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˈkʌl.tʃə ˌʃɒk</span>/</span></span> </div>
<div class="pos-body">
<div class="pr dsense dsense-noh">
<div class="cid"></div>
<div class="sense-body dsense_b">
<div class="def-block ddef_block">
<div class="ddef_h">
<div class="def ddef_d db">a <a class="query" title="feeling" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/feeling">feeling</a> of <a class="query" title="confusion" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/confusion">confusion</a> <a class="query" title="felt" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/felt">felt</a> by someone <a class="query" title="visiting" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/visiting">visiting</a> a <a class="query" title="country" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/country">country</a> or <a class="query" title="place" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/place">place</a> that they do not <a class="query" title="know" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/know">know</a></div>
<div class="def ddef_d db"> </div>
<div class="def ddef_d db">As an American living in Paris, I'm not exactly sure when I first started having moments of culture shock on my visits back to the US.</div>
<div class="def ddef_d db">From:  https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/culture-shock</div>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50433&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Leonela Handanović" aria-label="Leonela Handanović" role="img">LH</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>curmudgeon</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50433&amp;course=12136">Leonela Handanović</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 3:17 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span class="pos"><strong><i>noun</i></strong></span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/help/codes.html">[<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><span class="gc">C</span><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">-countable noun</span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>]</a></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="usage">old-fashioned</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="region"><strong> UK</strong></span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><span class="pron">/</span><span class="ipa">kəˈmʌdʒ.</span><span class="sp">ə</span><span class="ipa">n</span><span class="pron">/</span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="region"><strong> US</strong></span><span class="apple-converted-space"> <span class="pron">/</span><span class="ipa">kɚˈmʌdʒ.</span><span class="sp">ə</span><span class="ipa">n</span><span class="pron">/</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong>an</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><a title="old" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/old"><strong>old</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><a title="person" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/person"><strong>person</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>who is often in a</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><a title="bad" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/bad"><strong>bad</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><a title="mood" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/mood"><strong>mood</strong></a></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">ENG: She'll be glad to get away from that old curmudgeon for a week.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">SLO: Vesela bo, da se bo za en teden rešila te stare tečnobe.</span></p>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>D</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=47211&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Sara Lesjak" aria-label="Sara Lesjak" role="img">SL</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>disjointed</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=47211&amp;course=12136">Sara Lesjak</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 9:16 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span class="pos">adjective</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="daud"> </span><span class="pron">/</span><span class="ipa">dɪsˈdʒɔɪn.tɪd</span><span class="pron">/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">(Especially of words or ideas) not well connected or well ordered.</p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="eg">Example: The </span>script<span class="eg"> was disjointed and hard to </span>follow<span class="eg">.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="eg">Translation: Scenarij je bil nepovezan in težko sledljiv.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/disjointed">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/disjointed</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: disjointed" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91245"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: disjointed" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: disjointed"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91245&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5fe862d" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5fe862d" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5fe862d">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5fe862d" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5fe862d" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5fe862d" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5fe862d" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5fe862d" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5fe862d"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5fe862d" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Maj Rengeo" aria-label="Maj Rengeo" role="img">MR</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>double-edged sword</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136">Maj Rengeo</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 3:26 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun, idiom</p>
<p><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">/</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ˌ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">d</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ʌ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">b<sup>ə</sup>l</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ˈ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ɛdʒd sɔ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ː</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">d/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">an event or phenomenon whose negative effect is inseparable from a positive one.</span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">Too much IT, however, can be a double-edged sword.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><em>Preveč IT-ja pa je lahko dvorezen meč.</em></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">From: https://www.collinsdictionary.com/us/dictionary/english/double-edged-sword</p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: double-edged sword" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90549"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: double-edged sword" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: double-edged sword"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90549&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5fe9699" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5fe9699" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5fe9699">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5fe9699" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5fe9699" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5fe9699" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5fe9699" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5fe9699" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5fe9699"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5fe9699" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="region"><strong> </strong></span><span class="region"><strong>UK</strong></span><span class="apple-converted-space">  </span><span class="pron">/</span><span class="ipa">ˌdaʊ.tɪŋ ˈtɒm.əs</span><span class="pron">/</span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">  </span></strong><span class="region"><strong>US</strong></span><span class="apple-converted-space">  </span><span class="pron">/</span><span class="ipa">ˌdaʊ.t̬ɪŋ ˈtɑː.məs</span><span class="pron">/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong>a</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>person</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>who</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>refuses</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>to</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>believe</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>anything until they are</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>shown </strong><strong>proof</strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">ENG</span></i><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">: </span>He’s such a<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><strong>doubting Thomas</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"> that he won’t believe unless he sees things through his eyes</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">SLO: On je tak nejeverni Tomaž, da ne bo verjel, dokler ne vidi stvari na lastne oči.</span></p>

<span class="uk dpron-i" style="font-size:1rem;"><span class="pron dpron">/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˈdrɪə.ri</span>/</span></span><span style="font-size:1rem;"> </span><span class="us dpron-i" style="font-size:1rem;"><span class="region dreg">us</span><span class="daud"> </span></span></div>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Manca Panjan" aria-label="Manca Panjan" role="img">MP</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Dunkirk spirit</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136">Manca Panjan</a> - Sunday, 16 November 2025, 9:59 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/<span class="ipa">ˈdʌnkɜːk ˌspɪr.ɪt</span>/</p>
<p><strong><span style="color:#000000;"><a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="willingness" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/willingness">Willingness</a> by a <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="group" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/group">group</a> of <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="people" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/people">people</a> who are in a <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="bad" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/bad">bad</a> <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="situation" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/situation">situation</a> to all <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="help" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/help">help</a> each other</span></strong></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">Example sentence: There was a <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="Dunkirk" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/dunkirk">Dunkirk</a> <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="spirit" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/spirit">spirit</a> in the <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="village" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/village">village</a> during the <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="floods" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/flood">floods</a>.</span></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">Translation: Med poplavami so vaščani stopili skupaj in si med seboj pomagali.</span></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">Source: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/dunkirk-spirit?q=Dunkirk+spirit">Dunkirk spirit | English meaning - Cambridge Dictionary</a></span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Dunkirk spirit" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90761"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Dunkirk spirit" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Dunkirk spirit"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90761&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff5feda1c" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff5feda1c" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff5feda1c">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff5feda1c" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff5feda1c" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff5feda1c" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff5feda1c" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff5feda1c" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff5feda1c"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff5feda1c" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50197&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Petja Božič" aria-label="Petja Božič" role="img">PB</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>egregiously</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50197&amp;course=12136">Petja Božič</a> - Monday, 10 November 2025, 7:00 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adverb </p>
<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ɪˈɡriː.dʒəs.li</span>/</p>
<p>in an extremely bad or noticeable way</p>

<p><span class="daud"> </span><span class="pron dpron">/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˌtɒm ˌdɪk ənd ˈhær.i</span>/</span></p>
<p><span class="pron dpron">used to refer to an ordinary person or all ordinary people</span></p>
<p><span class="pron dpron">This was not information for every Tom, Dick, and Harry to have access to.</span></p>
<p><span class="pron dpron">To ni bila informacija za slehernega.</span></p>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>F</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53416&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Luka Fijavž Vivod" aria-label="Luka Fijavž Vivod" role="img">LF</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>factitious</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53416&amp;course=12136">Luka Fijavž Vivod</a> - Monday, 10 November 2025, 6:18 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adjective </p>
<p>/fækˈtɪʃ.əs/</p>
<p>(formal)<strong> artificial rather than natural:</strong></p>
<p><em>The excitement was largely factitious and confined to the media.</em></p>
<p><em>Navdušenje je bilo v veliki meri izumetničeno in omejeno na medije. </em></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50197&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Petja Božič" aria-label="Petja Božič" role="img">PB</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Fair game</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50197&amp;course=12136">Petja Božič</a> - Sunday, 21 December 2025, 10:23 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun</p>
<p><span class="daud"> </span><span class="pron dpron">/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˌfeə ˈɡeɪm</span>/</span></p>
<div class="row entry-header">
<div class="col-12">
<div class="entry-header-content d-flex flex-wrap align-items-baseline flex-row mb-0"> </div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ul-must-login-def">
<div></div>
</div>
<div class="vg">
<div class="vg-sseq-entry-item">
<div class="sb no-sn ms-lg-4 ms-3 w-100">
<div class="sb-0 sb-entry">
<div class="sense no-subnum">
<div class="sense-content w-100"><span class="dtText">someone or something that can be chased, attacked, or criticized</span></div>
<div class="sense-content w-100"> </div>
<div class="sense-content w-100"><span class="dtText">There's no radicalism in finding new ways to perpetuate a culture in which we're all fair game for judgement.</span></div>
<div class="sense-content w-100"><span class="dtText">From:  https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/fair-game</span></div>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53969&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Neli Orešek" aria-label="Neli Orešek" role="img">NO</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>from pillar to post</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53969&amp;course=12136">Neli Orešek</a> - Tuesday, 23 December 2025, 9:54 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/frɒm ˈpɪlə tə pəʊst/</p>
<p>Forced to keep moving from one place to another.</p>
<p>My parents were always on the move and so my childhood was spent being dragged <em>from pillar to post.</em></p>
<p>Moji starši so bili vedno potujoči, zato sem otroštvo preživela vlečena sem ter tja.</p>
<p>Source: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/from-pillar-to-post">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/from-pillar-to-post</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: from pillar to post" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91260"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: from pillar to post" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: from pillar to post"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91260&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff60050cf" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff60050cf" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff60050cf">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff60050cf" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff60050cf" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff60050cf" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff60050cf" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff60050cf" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff60050cf"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff60050cf" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=54239&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Valentina Mavrič" aria-label="Valentina Mavrič" role="img">VM</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>gaslighting</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=54239&amp;course=12136">Valentina Mavrič</a> - Sunday, 9 November 2025, 11:51 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun</p>
<p>/ˈɡæslaɪtɪŋ/</p>
<p>the action of tricking or controlling someone by making them believe things that are not true, especially by suggesting that they may be mentally ill</p>
<p>Gaslighting is a form of psychological abuse.</p>
<p>Mračenje je oblika psihičnega nasilja.</p>
<p>Source: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/gaslighting</p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: gaslighting" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90567"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: gaslighting" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: gaslighting"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90567&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6006328" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6006328" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6006328">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6006328" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6006328" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6006328" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6006328" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6006328" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6006328"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6006328" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Manca Panjan" aria-label="Manca Panjan" role="img">MP</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>gratuity</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136">Manca Panjan</a> - Friday, 19 December 2025, 7:28 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun</p>
<p>/ɡrəˈtjuːəti/</p>
<p><strong>(formal) Money that you give to somebody who has provided a service for you</strong></p>
<p>Synonym: tip</p>
<p>Example sentence: <span class="x">Our staff may not accept gratuities.</span></p>
<p><span class="x">Translation: Naše osebje ne sme sprejemati napitnin.</span></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53905&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Luca Marinko" aria-label="Luca Marinko" role="img">LM</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>have nothing to lose</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53905&amp;course=12136">Luca Marinko</a> - Tuesday, 2 December 2025, 1:28 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p><span class="TextRun SCXW215800582 BCX0" lang="en-us" xml:lang="en-us"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW215800582 BCX0">/</span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW215800582 BCX0">hæv</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW215800582 BCX0"> ˈ</span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW215800582 BCX0">nʌθɪŋ</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW215800582 BCX0"> </span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW215800582 BCX0">tu</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW215800582 BCX0">ː </span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW215800582 BCX0">l</span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW215800582 BCX0">uːz</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW215800582 BCX0">/</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW215800582 BCX0"> </span></p>
<div class="OutlineElement Ltr SCXW229817370 BCX0">
<p class="Paragraph SCXW229817370 BCX0" xml:lang="en-us" lang="en-us"><strong><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW229817370 BCX0">to be in a situation that could improve by doing something and that will not be any worse if you fail at it</span><span class="EOP SCXW229817370 BCX0"> </span></strong></p>
</div>
<div class="OutlineElement Ltr SCXW229817370 BCX0">
<p class="Paragraph SCXW229817370 BCX0" xml:lang="en-us" lang="en-us"><span class="TextRun SCXW229817370 BCX0" lang="en-us" xml:lang="en-us"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW229817370 BCX0">E.g. <em><span style="color:#7d9fd3;">He had nothing to lose, so he accepted the offer</span></em></span><em><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW229817370 BCX0" style="color:#7d9fd3;">.</span></em></span><em><span class="EOP SCXW229817370 BCX0" style="color:#7d9fd3;"> </span></em></p>
<p class="Paragraph SCXW229817370 BCX0" xml:lang="en-us" lang="en-us"><span class="EOP SCXW229817370 BCX0" style="color:#000000;">Slovenian translation: <span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>Ničesar ni imel izgubuti, zato je sprejel ponudbo. </em></span></span></p>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>I</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Špela Švab" aria-label="Špela Švab" role="img">ŠŠ</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>imminent</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136">Špela Švab</a> - Monday, 3 November 2025, 7:53 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p style="line-height:1;">adjective</p>
<p style="line-height:1;">/<span class="ipa">ˈɪm.ɪ.nənt</span>/</p>
<p style="line-height:1;"><span style="color:#000000;"><strong>Coming or<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="likely" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/likely"><strong>likely</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>to<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="happen" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/happen"><strong>happen</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>very<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="soon" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/soon"><strong>soon.</strong></a></span></p>
<p class="eg" style="line-height:1;"><span style="color:#000000;">For a man in imminent<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="danger" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/danger">danger</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>of<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="losing" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/losing">losing</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>his<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="job" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/job">job</a>, he<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="appeared" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/appear">appeared</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="quite" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/quite">quite</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="unruffled" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/unruffled">unruffled</a>.</span></p>
<p style="line-height:1;">Za nekoga, ki mu je grozila skorajšnja izguba službe, je deloval precej mirno.</p>
<p style="line-height:1;">From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/imminent">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/imminent</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: imminent" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90554"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: imminent" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: imminent"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90554&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff600af0a" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff600af0a" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff600af0a">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff600af0a" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff600af0a" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff600af0a" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff600af0a" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff600af0a" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff600af0a"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff600af0a" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>
