<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Hana Bric" aria-label="Hana Bric" role="img">HB</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>incessant</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136">Hana Bric</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 3:14 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">Adjective </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">/</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">n</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ˈ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">ses.ənt/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">never </span></strong><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb"><a title="stopping" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/stopping"><strong><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">stopping</span></strong></a><strong>, </strong><a title="especially" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/especially"><strong><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">especially</span></strong></a><strong> in an </strong><a title="annoying" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/annoy"><strong><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">annoying</span></strong></a><strong> or </strong><a title="unpleasant" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/unpleasant"><strong><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">unpleasant</span></strong></a><strong> way:</strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">incessant <a title="rain" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/rain"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">rain</span></a>/<a title="noise" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/noise"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">noise</span></a>/<a title="complaints" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/complaint"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">complaints</span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">nenehen, neprekinjen dež/hrup | nenehne, neprekinjene pritožbe</span></p>

<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ɪnˈtæn.dʒə.b<span class="sp dsp">ə</span>l</span>/</p>
<p><strong>impossible to touch, describe exactly, or to give an exact value:</strong></p>
<p>Example: She has that intangible quality which you might call charisma.</p>
<p>Translation: Ima to nedoumljivo lastnost, ki bi ji lahko rekli karizma.</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53416&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Luka Fijavž Vivod" aria-label="Luka Fijavž Vivod" role="img">LF</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>invidiously</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53416&amp;course=12136">Luka Fijavž Vivod</a> - Monday, 24 November 2025, 5:30 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adverb</p>
<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ɪnˈvɪd.i.əs.li</span>/</p>
<p>(formal) <strong>In a way that is likely to cause unhappiness or be unpleasant, especially because of being unfair:</strong></p>
<p><em>It is not ethical to take a benefit that is<strong> indiviously </strong>denied to other people.</em></p>
<p><em>Ni etično izkoristiti ugodnosti, ki je drugim ljudem krivično odtegnjena.</em></p>
<p>From:<a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/invidiously">INVIDIOUSLY | English meaning - Cambridge Dictionary</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: invidiously" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90816"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: invidiously" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: invidiously"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90816&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff600eb73" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff600eb73" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff600eb73">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff600eb73" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff600eb73" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff600eb73" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff600eb73" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff600eb73" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff600eb73"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff600eb73" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Katarina Dimitrijević" aria-label="Katarina Dimitrijević" role="img">KD</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Irish goodbye</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136">Katarina Dimitrijević</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 7:49 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p><strong>/ˈaɪrɪʃ ɡʊdˈbaɪ/</strong></p>
<p>An <em>Irish goodbye</em> is when you abruptly leave a party (or other social event) without telling anyone.</p>
<p>e.g. “Close the door! I’m doing <span style="color:#7d9fd3;">an Irish goodbye</span>!” she says. </p>
<p>Translation: »Zapri vrata! <span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><strong>Zbrišem jo</strong></span>!« je rekla.</p>
<p>From: <a href="https://www.dictionary.com/e/slang/irish-goodbye/">https://www.dictionary.com/e/slang/irish-goodbye/</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Irish goodbye" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90664"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Irish goodbye" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Irish goodbye"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90664&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff600f930" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff600f930" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff600f930">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">1</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff600f930" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff600f930" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff600f930" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff600f930" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff600f930" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff600f930"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff600f930" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>J</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Hana Bric" aria-label="Hana Bric" role="img">HB</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Jump the gun</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136">Hana Bric</a> - Monday, 15 December 2025, 10:03 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">/'dʒ<span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;">ʌ</span>mp ðə '<span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;">ɡʌ</span>n/</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">To do something too <a title="soon" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/soon"><span style="text-decoration:none;">soon</span></a>, <a title="especially" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/especially"><span style="text-decoration:none;">especially</span></a> without <a title="thinking" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/thinking"><span style="text-decoration:none;">thinking</span></a> <a title="carefully" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/carefully"><span style="text-decoration:none;">carefully</span></a> about it.</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">e.g. They've only just <a title="met" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/met"><span style="text-decoration:none;">met</span></a> - isn't it <a title="jumping" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/jump"><span style="text-decoration:none;">jumping</span></a> the <a title="gun" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/gun"><span style="text-decoration:none;">gun</span></a> to be <a title="talking" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/talk"><span style="text-decoration:none;">talking</span></a> about <a title="marriage" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/marriage"><span style="text-decoration:none;">marriage</span></a> already?</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Translation: Šele spoznala sta se, ali ni prezgodaj za pogovor o poroki?</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/jump-the-gun">JUMP THE GUN | English meaning - Cambridge Dictionary</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Jump the gun" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91118"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Jump the gun" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Jump the gun"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91118&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6010927" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6010927" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6010927">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6010927" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6010927" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6010927" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6010927" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6010927" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6010927"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6010927" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>K</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=17307&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><img src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/pluginfile.php/126624/user/icon/boost_union_ff/f2?rev=3775940" class="userpicture" width="35" height="35" alt="Kristina Gregorčič" title="Kristina Gregorčič" /></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>keep up with the Joneses</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=17307&amp;course=12136">Kristina Gregorčič</a> - Wednesday, 24 September 2025, 9:37 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p dir="ltr">idiom</p>
<p dir="ltr">/kiːp ʌp wɪð ðə ˈdʒəʊnzɪz/</p>
<p><strong>If you say that someone is keeping up with the <span class="highlight">Joneses</span>, you mean that they are doing something in order to show that they have as much money as other people, rather than because they really want to do it.</strong></p>
<p><em>Many people were holding down three jobs just to keep up with the <span class="highlight">Joneses</span>.</em></p>
<p><em>Številni so opravljali po tri službe, da so lahko tekmovali s sosedi.<br /><br /></em>From: <a href="https://www.collinsdictionary.com/dictionary/english/keep-up-with-the-joneses">https://www.collinsdictionary.com/dictionary/english/keep-up-with-the-<span class="highlight">joneses</span></a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span <p class="Paragraph SCXW40735532 BCX0" xml:lang="en-us" lang="en-us"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0">Slovenian translation: </span><span class="TextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0" lang="en-us" xml:lang="en-us"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0">Program </span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW40735532 BCX0">recikliranja</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0"> je </span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW40735532 BCX0">hvalevreden</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0">, </span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW40735532 BCX0">ampak</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0"> </span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW40735532 BCX0">ali</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0"> </span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW40735532 BCX0">prihrani</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0"> </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0">kaj</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0"> </span><span class="NormalTextRun SpellingErrorV2Themed SCXW40735532 BCX0">denarja</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW40735532 BCX0">?</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW40735532 BCX0"> </span></p>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>M</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Brina Mohar" aria-label="Brina Mohar" role="img">BM</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>magnum opus</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136">Brina Mohar</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 11:15 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun</p>
<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˌmæɡ.nəm ˈəʊ.pəs</span>/</p>
<div class="ddef_h">
<div class="def ddef_d db">the most important piece of work done by a writer or artist</div>
<div class="def ddef_d db"> </div>
</div>
<div class="def-body ddef_b">
<div class="examp dexamp"><span class="eg deg">Picasso's Guernica is considered by many to be his magnum opus.</span></div>
<div class="examp dexamp"> </div>
<div class="examp dexamp"><span class="eg deg">Mnogi menijo, da je Guernica Picassovo najpomembnejše delo.</span></div>
<div class="examp dexamp"> </div>
<div class="examp dexamp"><span class="eg deg">From: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/magnum-opus</span></div>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50997&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Miha Kolenc" aria-label="Miha Kolenc" role="img">MK</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>modus operandi</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50997&amp;course=12136">Miha Kolenc</a> - Monday, 15 December 2025, 9:07 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun</p>
<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˌməʊ.dəs ˌɒp.əˈræn.diː</span>/</p>
<p><strong>(<span style="color:#7d9fd3;">formal</span>) a distinct pattern or method of operation that indicates or suggests the work of a single criminal in more than one crime</strong></p>
<p>example: A serial killer's modus operandi can evolve as they gain experience or grow older.</p>
<p>translation: Način delovanja serijskega morilca se lahko spreminja, s tem ko pridobiva izkušnje ali se stara.</p>
<p>from: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/modus-operandi</p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: modus operandi" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91078"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: modus operandi" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: modus operandi"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91078&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff601c6da" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff601c6da" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff601c6da">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff601c6da" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff601c6da" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff601c6da" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff601c6da" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff601c6da" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff601c6da"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff601c6da" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Brina Mohar" aria-label="Brina Mohar" role="img">BM</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>moribund</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136">Brina Mohar</a> - Monday, 3 November 2025, 11:32 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="text-indent:-18pt;text-align:left;"><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Symbol;" xml:lang="en-gb">·<span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman';">        </span></span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">adjective</span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="text-indent:-18pt;text-align:left;padding-left:40px;"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb"><span lang="en-gb" style="font-size:11pt;line-height:107%;font-family:Calibri, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">/ 'mɒrɪbʌnd/</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="text-indent:-18pt;text-align:left;padding-left:40px;"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb"><span lang="en-gb" style="font-size:11pt;line-height:107%;font-family:Calibri, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">especially of organization or business, not active or successful (Cambridge Dictionary)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">How can the department be revived from its present <strong>moribund </strong>state? (Cambridge Dictionary)</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">Kako bi lahko oddelek obudili iz njegovega trenutnega <strong>umirajočega</strong> stanja?</span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: moribund" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90562"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: moribund" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: moribund"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90562&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff601d8af" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff601d8af" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff601d8af">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff601d8af" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff601d8af" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff601d8af" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff601d8af" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff601d8af" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff601d8af"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff601d8af" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Manca Panjan" aria-label="Manca Panjan" role="img">MP</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>mounting</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136">Manca Panjan</a> - Sunday, 9 November 2025, 8:54 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adjective</p>
<p>/ˈmaʊntɪŋ/</p>
<p><strong>increasing, often in a manner that causes or expresses worry</strong></p>
<p>Example sentence: <span class="x">In the face of mounting pressure, the president decided to act.</span></p>
<p><span class="x">Translation: Zaradi vse večjega pritiska se je predsednik odločil ukrepati.</span></p>

<p><span class="Apple-converted-space"> </span>/ˈmʌs.tər/</p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;"><strong><a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/produce">To produce</a> or <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/encourage">encourage</a> something such as an <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/emotion">emotion</a> or <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/support">support.</a></strong></span></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53747&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Rebeka Košir" aria-label="Rebeka Košir" role="img">RK</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>nervous Nelly</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53747&amp;course=12136">Rebeka Košir</a> - Sunday, 21 December 2025, 12:38 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>Idiom</p>
<p>/ˈnɜːvəs ˈnɛlɪ/</p>
<p>a person or animal that tends to be timid or anxious</p>
<p>My sister is a real nervous Nellie when it comes to flying.</p>

<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">/</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-size:11.5pt;line-height:107%;font-family:Helvetica, sans-serif;color:#373737;background:#FFFFFF;" xml:lang="en-gb"> </span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">w</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ʊ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">d n</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɒ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">t <a href="https://tophonetics.com/"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">du</span><span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">ː</span></a> </span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ˈ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">s</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ʌ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">mθ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ŋ fɔ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ː</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">r ɔ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ː</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">l ðə ti</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ː</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb"> </span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">n </span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ˈʧ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">a</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">nə/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span style="color:#000000;">used to say that nothing could <a title="persuade" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/persuade"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">persuade</span></a> you to do something:</span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color:#000000;">I wouldn't take that <a title="job" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/job"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">job</span></a> for all the <a title="tea" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/tea"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">tea</span></a> in <a title="China" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/china"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">China</span></a>.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color:#000000;">Tega dela ne bi sprejel pod nobenim pogojem. </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color:#000000;">From: </span><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb"><a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/would-not-do-for-all-the-tea-in-china?q=not+for+all+the+tea+in+china">would not do something for all the tea in China - Cambridge English Dictionary</a></span><span style="color:#000000;"> </span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: not for all the tea in China" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90778"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: not for all the tea in China" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: not for all the tea in China"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90778&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6022fed" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6022fed" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6022fed">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6022fed" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6022fed" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6022fed" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6022fed" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6022fed" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6022fed"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6022fed" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>O</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Manca Panjan" aria-label="Manca Panjan" role="img">MP</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>obsolescence</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136">Manca Panjan</a> - Sunday, 21 December 2025, 2:27 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">noun</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">/ˌɒbsəˈlesəns/</span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle"><strong><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">(Formal) The process or fact becoming old-fashioned and no longer useful</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb"> </span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">Example sentence: Unless it changes, the industry faces the risk of technological obsolescence.</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">Translation: </span>Če ne bo prišlo do sprememb, industriji grozi tehnološka zastarelost. </p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">Source:</span> <span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb"><a <table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53969&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Neli Orešek" aria-label="Neli Orešek" role="img">NO</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>opaque</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53969&amp;course=12136">Neli Orešek</a> - Tuesday, 23 December 2025, 9:30 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adjective</p>
<p>/əʊˈpeɪk/</p>
<p>Preventing light from travelling through, and therefore not transparent or translucent.</p>
<p><em>Opaque</em> writing or speech is difficult to understand.</p>
<p>Nejasno pisanje ali govor je težko razumeti.</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Maj Rengeo" aria-label="Maj Rengeo" role="img">MR</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>over your head</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136">Maj Rengeo</a> - Monday, 24 November 2025, 8:08 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">/</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ˈəʊvə jɔː hɛd</span><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">too difficult or strange for you to understand.</span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">I tried to take in what he was saying about nuclear fusion, but most of it went over my head.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">Poskušal sem dojeti, kaj je govoril o jedrski fuziji, vendar mi je bila večina nedoumljiva.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">From: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/over-head</span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: over your head" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90819"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: over your head" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: over your head"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90819&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6029bcf" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6029bcf" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6029bcf">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6029bcf" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6029bcf" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6029bcf" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6029bcf" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6029bcf" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6029bcf"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6029bcf" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>P</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Špela Švab" aria-label="Špela Švab" role="img">ŠŠ</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>paradoxical</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136">Špela Švab</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 3:13 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adjective</p>
<p> /ˌpær.əˈdɒk.sɪ.kəl/</p>
<p><strong><span style="color:#000000;"><a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/seeming">Seeming</a> <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/impossible">impossible</a> or <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/difficult">difficult</a> to <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/understand">understand</a> because of <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/contain">containing</a> two <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/opposite">opposite</a> <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/fact">facts</a> or <a style="color:#000000;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/characteristic">characteristics</a>.</span></strong></p>
<p>It seems paradoxical to me, but if you drink a cup of hot tea it seems to cool you down.</p>
<p>Zveni protislovno, ampak če popiješ skodelico vročega čaja, te na nek<span style="color:#da261b;"><span style="text-decoration:underline;">i</span> </span>način ohladi.</p>
<p>Source: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/paradoxical">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/paradoxical</a></p>
<p></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50997&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Miha Kolenc" aria-label="Miha Kolenc" role="img">MK</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>paraphilia</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50997&amp;course=12136">Miha Kolenc</a> - Sunday, 14 December 2025, 10:27 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="p1">noun</p>
<p class="p1">/ˌparəˈfɪliə/</p>
<p class="p1"><strong> a pattern of recurring sexually arousing mental imagery or behavior that involves unusual and especially socially unacceptable sexual practices (such as sadism or pedophilia)</strong></p>
<p class="p1">example: More commonly discussed types of <em>paraphilia </em>are things like pedophilia, zoophilia, and objectophilia.</p>
<p class="p1">translation: Bolj pogoste vrste parafilije so pedofilija, zoofilija in objektofilija.</p>

<p></p>
<p>a man who tries to secretly watch women when they are wearing no clothes</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Hana Bric" aria-label="Hana Bric" role="img">HB</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>plaintive</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136">Hana Bric</a> - Tuesday, 18 November 2025, 12:54 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">Adjective</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">UK: /</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ˈ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">ple</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">n.t</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">v/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">US: /</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ˈ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">ple</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">n.t</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">̬ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">v/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">used to </span></strong><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb"><a title="describe" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/describe"><strong><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">describe</span></strong></a><strong> something that </strong><a title="sounds" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/sound"><strong><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">sounds</span></strong></a><strong> </strong><a title="slightly" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/slightly"><strong><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">slightly</span></strong></a><strong> </strong><a title="sad" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/sad"><strong><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">sad</span></strong></a><strong>:</strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">the plaintive <a title="sound" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/sound"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">sound</span></a> of the <a title="bagpipes" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/bagpipes"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">bagpipes</span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">"What about me?" came a plaintive <a title="voice" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/voice"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">voice</span></a>.</span></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53398&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Luka Segečić" aria-label="Luka Segečić" role="img">LS</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>poisoned chalice</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53398&amp;course=12136">Luka Segečić</a> - Monday, 3 November 2025, 4:04 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p></p>
<p>/ˌpɔɪ.zənd ˈtʃæl.ɪs/</p>
<p></p>
<p>Something that seems very good when it is first received, but in fact does great harm to the person who receives it.</p>
<p></p>
<p><em>The leadership of the party turned out to be a poisoned chalice.</em></p>
<p></p>
<p><em>Vodstvo stranke se je izkazalo za slabo, čeprav se je zdelo dobro.</em></p>
<p></p>
<p><em>From: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/poisoned-chalice</em></p>
<p></p>
<p><em>Luka Segečić </em></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: poisoned chalice" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90533"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: poisoned chalice" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: poisoned chalice"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90533&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff602fe3b" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff602fe3b" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff602fe3b">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff602fe3b" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff602fe3b" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff602fe3b" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff602fe3b" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff602fe3b" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff602fe3b"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff602fe3b" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb"> </span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">/prɪˈkeəriəs/</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle"><strong><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">​(of a situation) not safe or certain; dangerous</span></strong><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">Example sentence: </span><i>T<span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">he world is a precarious and unstable place.</span></i><i></i> </p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Maj Rengeo" aria-label="Maj Rengeo" role="img">MR</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>put your money where your mouth is</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136">Maj Rengeo</a> - Sunday, 9 November 2025, 11:55 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">/p</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ʊ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">t jɔ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ː</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si"> </span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ˈ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">m</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ʌ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ni weə jɔ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ː</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si"> ma</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ʊ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">θ </span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ɪ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">z/</span></p>
<p><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si"><strong>to give practical support to causes or activities that you believe are right, especially by giving money.</strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">If the minister is so keen on the school he should put his money where his mouth is and give us more resources.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">Če je minister tako navdušen nad šolo, bi moral <strong><span style="color:#da261b;">izpolniti svoje obljube</span></strong> in nam dati več sredstev.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si"><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">From: https://www.collinsdictionary.com/us/dictionary/english/put-your-money-where-your-mouth-is</span></span></p>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>R</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Hana Bric" aria-label="Hana Bric" role="img">HB</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>rack something up (1)</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136">Hana Bric</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 5:00 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">idiom</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">/ræk ʌp/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">to <a title="gradually" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/gradually"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">gradually</span></a> get more <a title="points" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/focus"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">points</span></a>, <a title="profits" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/profit"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">profits</span></a>, etc.:</span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">He has <a title="racked" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/rack"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">racked</span></a> up 450 <a title="points" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/focus"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">points</span></a> in three <a title="months" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/month"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">months</span></a>.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">V treh mesecih je zbral 450 točk.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/rack-up?q=to+rack+up">RACK SOMETHING UP | English meaning - Cambridge Dictionary</a></span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: rack something up (1)" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90777"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: rack something up (1)" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: rack something up (1)"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90777&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6034387" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6034387" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6034387">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6034387" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6034387" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6034387" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6034387" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6034387" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6034387"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6034387" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>
 </td></tr></table>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53398&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Luka Segečić" aria-label="Luka Segečić" role="img">LS</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>reach an impasse</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53398&amp;course=12136">Luka Segečić</a> - Tuesday, 23 December 2025, 9:50 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>/<span class="fr_norm">riːʧ</span> <span class="fr_norm">ən</span> <span class="fr_norm">æmˈpɑːs</span>/</p>
<p>To get to a situation in which progress is impossible, especially because the people involved cannot agree<br /><br /><em>The dispute had reached an impasse, as neither side would compromise.</em></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53969&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Neli Orešek" aria-label="Neli Orešek" role="img">NO</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>reciprocity</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53969&amp;course=12136">Neli Orešek</a> - Tuesday, 23 December 2025, 9:00 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun</p>
<p>/res.ɪˈprɒs.ə.ti/</p>
<p>Behaviour in which two people or groups of people give each other help and advantages.</p>
<p>We offer to all our trading partners a commitment to reciprocity and fairness.<br />Vsem našim trgovinskim partnerjem ponujamo zavezanost vzajemnosti in pravičnosti.</p>
<p>Source: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/reciprocity">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/reciprocity</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: reciprocity" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91254"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: reciprocity" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: reciprocity"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91254&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff60363fd" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff60363fd" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff60363fd">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff60363fd" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff60363fd" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff60363fd" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff60363fd" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff60363fd" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff60363fd"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff60363fd" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=47211&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Sara Lesjak" aria-label="Sara Lesjak" role="img">SL</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>repudiation</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=47211&amp;course=12136">Sara Lesjak</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 11:30 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span class="pos">noun</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"> <span class="daud"> <span class="pron">/<span class="ipa">rɪˌpjuː.diˈeɪ.ʃ<span class="sp">ə</span></span><span class="ipa">n</span></span><span class="pron">/</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">The act of refusing to accept something or someone as true, good, or reasonable.</p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="eg">Example: They were surprised by his sudden repudiation <span class="b">of</span><span class="eg"> all his former beliefs.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="eg">Translation: Njegova nenadna zavrnitev vseh svojih prejšnjih prepričanj jih je presenetila.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/repudiation">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/repudiation</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: repudiation" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91242"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: repudiation" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: repudiation"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91242&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff60374f5" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff60374f5" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff60374f5">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff60374f5" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff60374f5" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff60374f5" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff60374f5" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff60374f5" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff60374f5"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff60374f5" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Nena Horvat" aria-label="Nena Horvat" role="img">NH</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Rip/tear up the rulebook</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136">Nena Horvat</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 10:50 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p><span style="font-size:1rem;">/rɪp / teər ʌp ðə ˈruːl.bʊk /</span></p>
<p>idiom</p>
<p>To do something in a way that is very different to the way in which it is usually done or has been done in the past.</p>
<p>The <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/book">book</a> <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/reveal">reveals</a> the <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/story">story</a> of how the <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/couple">couple</a> <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/tore">tore</a> up the <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/rulebook">rulebook</a> and <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/create">created</a> <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/completely">completely</a> new <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/method">methods</a> of <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/brew">brewing</a><a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/beer">beer</a>.</p>
<p>Knjiga razkriva zgodbo o tem, kako par ni igral po pravilih in ustvaril čisto nove metode varjenja piva.</p>
<p>Source: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/rip-tear-up-the-rulebook?q=tear+up+the+rulebook">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/rip-tear-up-the-rulebook?q=tear+up+the+rulebook</a></p>
<p> </p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Rip/tear up the rulebook" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91237"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Rip/tear up the rulebook" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Rip/tear up the rulebook"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91237&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6038650" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6038650" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6038650">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6038650" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6038650" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6038650" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6038650" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6038650" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6038650"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6038650" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Filip-Lars Topolak" aria-label="Filip-Lars Topolak" role="img">FT</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>run of the mill</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136">Filip-Lars Topolak</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 6:07 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">adjective</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">UK /</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ˌ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">r</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ʌ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">n.əv.ðə</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ˈ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">m</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">l/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">US /</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ˌ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">r</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ʌ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">n.əv.ðə</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ˈ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">m</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ɪ</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">l/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">ordinary and not special or exciting in any way:</span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><i><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">He gave a fairly <strong>run-of-the-mill</strong> speech.</span></i></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><i>Imel je precej <strong>povprečen</strong> govor.</i></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">From: (<a <div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>S</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Filip-Lars Topolak" aria-label="Filip-Lars Topolak" role="img">FT</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>safe haven</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136">Filip-Lars Topolak</a> - Sunday, 16 November 2025, 5:13 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>noun</p>
<p>UK  /ˌseɪf ˈheɪ.vən/<br />US /ˌseɪf ˈheɪ.vən/</p>
<p><strong>a place where you are protected from harm or danger:</strong></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>As long as the UN soldiers were present, the city was regarded as a <strong>safe haven</strong> for the refugees.</em></span></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;">Dokler so bili tam prisotni vojaki OZN, je mesto veljalo za <strong>varno zatočišče</strong> za begunce.</span></p>
<p>From: (<a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/safe-haven">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/safe-haven</a>)</p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td <table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Katarina Dimitrijević" aria-label="Katarina Dimitrijević" role="img">KD</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Scale back/down (something)</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136">Katarina Dimitrijević</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 3:23 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>phrasal verb</p>
<p>/ˈskeɪl bæk ˈsʌmθɪŋ/ or /ˈskeɪl daʊn ˈsʌmθɪŋ/</p>
<p>To reduce something in size, amount, or production: </p>
<p>e.g. <span class="eg deg">Sid will have to <em><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><strong>scale back</strong></span></em> his plans. </span></p>
<p></p>
<p>Translation: »Sid bo moral <em><strong><span style="color:#7d9fd3;">zmanjšati</span></strong></em> svoje načrte.«</p>
<div>
<div>From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/scale-back-down">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/scale-back-down</a></div>

<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˈskruː.tɪ.ni</span>/</p>
<p>the careful and detailed examination of something in order to get information about it</p>
<p>The government's record will come under scrutiny in the weeks before election.</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Manca Panjan" aria-label="Manca Panjan" role="img">MP</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>send somebody to Coventry</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136">Manca Panjan</a> - Monday, 15 December 2025, 10:28 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/send ˈsʌmbədi tə kɒvəntri/</p>
<p><strong><span style="color:#000000;">If a <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="group" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/group">group</a> of <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="people" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/people">people</a> <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="sends" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/send">sends</a> someone to Coventry, they <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="refuse" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/refuse">refuse</a> to <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="speak" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/speak">speak</a> to that <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="person" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/person">person</a>, usually as a <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="punishment" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/punish">punishment</a> for having done something to <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="upset" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/upset">upset</a> the <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="group" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/group">group</a></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">Example sentence: When she <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="returned" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/returned">returned</a> <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="home" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/home">home</a> her <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="mother" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/mother">mother</a> and <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="father" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/father">father</a> <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="sent" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/sent">sent</a> her to Coventry.</span></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">Translation: Ko se je vrnila domov, sta jo mama in oče ignorirala.</span></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">Source: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/send-to-coventry?q=send+somebody+to+Coventry </span></p>
