<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Špela Švab" aria-label="Špela Švab" role="img">ŠŠ</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>set the Thames on fire</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136">Špela Švab</a> - Monday, 3 November 2025, 7:38 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p style="line-height:1;">idiom</p>
<p style="line-height:1;">/<span class="ipa">set</span><span class="ipa"> ðə <span style="color:#000000;">temz</span></span> ɒn faɪə/</p>
<p style="line-height:1;"><span style="color:#000000;"><strong>To<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="cause" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/cause"><strong>cause</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>a lot of<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="excitement" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/excite"><strong>excitement</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>or<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="strong" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/strong"><strong>strong</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><a style="color:#000000;" title="feelings" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/feeling"><strong>feelings.</strong></a></span></p>
<p style="line-height:1;"><span style="color:#000000;">His<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="books" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/books">books</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="sell" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/sell">sell</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="fairly" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/fairly">fairly</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>well, but they don't<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="exactly" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/exactly">exactly</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>set the Thames on<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a style="color:#000000;" title="fire" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/fire">fire</a>.</span></p>
<p style="line-height:1;">Njegove knjige se precej dobro prodajajo, vendar niso ravno spektakularne.</p>
<p style="line-height:1;">From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/set-the-thames-on-fire">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/set-the-thames-on-fire</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: set the Thames on fire" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90552"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: set the Thames on fire" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: set the Thames on fire"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90552&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff603fcde" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff603fcde" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff603fcde">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff603fcde" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff603fcde" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff603fcde" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff603fcde" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff603fcde" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff603fcde"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff603fcde" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53398&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Luka Segečić" aria-label="Luka Segečić" role="img">LS</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>soft power</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53398&amp;course=12136">Luka Segečić</a> - Monday, 3 November 2025, 4:05 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/'soft pauə/</p>
<p></p>
<p>the use of a country's cultural and economic influence to persuade other countries to do something, rather than the use of military power</p>
<p></p>
<p><em>When it comes to soft power, Germany is now one of the most powerful nations on earth</em></p>
<p><em>Ko gre za mehko moč, je Nemčija zdaj ena najmočnejših držav na svetu.</em></p>
<p>from: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/soft-power</p>
<p>Luka Segečić </p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: soft power" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90534"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: soft power" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: soft power"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90534&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6042eec" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6042eec" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6042eec">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6042eec" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6042eec" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6042eec" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6042eec" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6042eec" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6042eec"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6042eec" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53416&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Luka Fijavž Vivod" aria-label="Luka Fijavž Vivod" role="img">LF</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>something hangs in the balance</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53416&amp;course=12136">Luka Fijavž Vivod</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 8:41 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/ˈsʌmθɪŋ hæŋz ɪn ðə ˈbæləns/</p>
<p><strong>It means that a result of a situation has not been decided yet.</strong></p>
<p><em>The game hang in the balance until the last seconds.</em></p>
<p><em>Tekma je visela na nitki do zadnjih sekund.</em></p>
<p>From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/hangs-in-the-balance">SOMETHING HANGS IN THE BALANCE - Cambridge English Dictionary</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: something hangs in the balance" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90538"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: something hangs in the balance" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: something hangs in the balance"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90538&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6043fcd" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6043fcd" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6043fcd">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6043fcd" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6043fcd" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6043fcd" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6043fcd" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6043fcd" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6043fcd"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6043fcd" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Brina Mohar" aria-label="Brina Mohar" role="img">BM</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>specious</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136">Brina Mohar</a> - Friday, 19 December 2025, 7:31 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adjective</p>
<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˈspiː.ʃəs</span>/</p>
<p>(formal) seeming to be right or true, but really wrong or false</p>
<div class="link">

<div class="def-block ddef_block">
<div class="def-body ddef_b">
<div class="examp dexamp"><span class="eg deg">His whole argument is specious.</span></div>
<div class="examp dexamp"> </div>
<div class="examp dexamp"><span class="eg deg">Cel njegov argument je varljiv.</span></div>
<div class="examp dexamp"> </div>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Maj Rengeo" aria-label="Maj Rengeo" role="img">MR</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Splurge</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136">Maj Rengeo</a> - Friday, 19 December 2025, 7:30 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>verb (informal)</p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">/spl</span><u><span lang="en-si" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ɜ</span></u><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">rdʒ/</span></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Filip-Lars Topolak" aria-label="Filip-Lars Topolak" role="img">FT</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>spoof</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136">Filip-Lars Topolak</a> - Monday, 15 December 2025, 10:47 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">noun</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">UK /spu</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ː</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">f/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">US /spu</span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">ː</span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">f/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">a funny and silly piece of writing, music, theatre, etc. that copies the style of an original work:</span></strong></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Manca Panjan" aria-label="Manca Panjan" role="img">MP</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>stamp out</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53959&amp;course=12136">Manca Panjan</a> - Sunday, 16 November 2025, 9:38 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>phrasal verb</p>
<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">stæmp aʊt</span>/</p>
<p><strong><span style="color:#000000;">To get <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="rid" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/rid">rid</a> of something that is <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="wrong" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/wrong">wrong</a> or <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="harmful" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/harm">harmful</a></span></strong></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">Example sentence: The new <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="legislation" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/legislation">legislation</a> is <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="intended" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/intended">intended</a> to <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="stamp" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/stamp">stamp</a> out <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="child" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/child">child</a> <a class="query" style="color:#000000;" title="prostitution" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/prostitution">prostitution</a>.</span></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">Translation: Nova zakonodaja naj bi odpravila otroško prostitucijo.</span></p>
<p><span style="color:#000000;">Source: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/stamp-out">STAMP SOMETHING OUT | English meaning - Cambridge Dictionary</a></span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: stamp out" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90759"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: stamp out" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: stamp out"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90759&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6048899" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6048899" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6048899">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6048899" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6048899" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6048899" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6048899" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6048899" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6048899"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6048899" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Katarina Dimitrijević" aria-label="Katarina Dimitrijević" role="img">KD</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Strike gold</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136">Katarina Dimitrijević</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 11:12 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/straɪk ˈɡəʊld/</p>
<p>To make large profits or to become rich:</p>
<p>e.g. A few lucky people have <span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><strong>struck gold </strong></span>by investing in this company.</p>
<p>Translation: Nekaj srečnih ljudi je z naložbami v to podjetje <span style="color:#7d9fd3;">zadelo zlato</span>.</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Nena Horvat" aria-label="Nena Horvat" role="img">NH</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Subversion</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136">Nena Horvat</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 1:58 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p><span style="font-size:1rem;">Noun</span></p>
<p>/səbˈvɜː.ʃən/</p>
<p>(Formal) The <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/act">act</a> of <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/trying">trying</a> to <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/destroy">destroy</a> or <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/damage">damage</a> an <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/established">established</a> <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/system">system</a> or <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/government">government</a>.</p>
<p>He was <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/found">found</a> <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/guilty">guilty</a> of subversion and <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/imprison">imprisoned</a>.</p>
<p>Spoznan je bil za krivega prevrata in poslan za zapahe.</p>
<p>Source: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/subversion">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/subversion</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Subversion" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90884"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Subversion" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Subversion"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90884&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff604dc4a" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff604dc4a" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff604dc4a">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff604dc4a" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff604dc4a" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff604dc4a" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff604dc4a" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff604dc4a" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff604dc4a"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff604dc4a" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>T</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Špela Švab" aria-label="Špela Švab" role="img">ŠŠ</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>take a back seat (to)</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53311&amp;course=12136">Špela Švab</a> - Monday, 3 November 2025, 7:50 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p style="line-height:1;">idiom</p>
<p style="line-height:1;">/teɪk ə <span class="ipa">ˌbæk ˈsiːt</span>/</p>
<p style="line-height:1;"><span style="color:#000000;"><strong>To<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="choose" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/choose"><strong>choose</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>not to be in a<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="position" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/position"><strong>position</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>of<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="responsibility" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/responsibility"><strong>responsibility</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>in an<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="organization" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/organization"><strong>organization</strong></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><strong> </strong></span><strong>or<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong><a style="color:#000000;" title="activity" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/activity"><strong>activity.</strong></a></span></p>
<p style="line-height:1;">In America, literal meanings take a backseat to more subjective associations.</p>
<p style="line-height:1;">V Ameriki dobesedni pomen pogosto stopi v ozadje pred bolj subjektivnimi asociacijami.</p>
<p style="line-height:1;">From: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/take-a-back-seat </p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: take a back seat (to)" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90553"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: take a back seat (to)" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: take a back seat (to)"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90553&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff604f157" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff604f157" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff604f157">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff604f157" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff604f157" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff604f157" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff604f157" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff604f157" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff604f157"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff604f157" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Filip-Lars Topolak" aria-label="Filip-Lars Topolak" role="img">FT</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>take on a life of its own</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53201&amp;course=12136">Filip-Lars Topolak</a> - Friday, 19 December 2025, 10:38 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p><span style="font-size:1rem;">idiom</span></p>
<p>/teɪk ɒn ə laɪf əv ɪts əʊn/</p>
<p><strong>to become very large, important, or hard to control:</strong></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>The story <strong>took on a life of its own</strong> and began to appear on news broadcasts everywhere.</em></span></p>
<p><span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>Zgodba <strong>je zaživela svoje življenje</strong> in se začela pojavljati v informativnih oddajah po vsem svetu.</em></span></p>
<p>From: (<a href="https://www.merriam-webster.com/dictionary/take%20on%20a%20life%20of%20its%20own">https://www.merriam-webster.com/dictionary/take%20on%20a%20life%20of%20its%20own</a><span <table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53551&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Lana Štimac" aria-label="Lana Štimac" role="img">LŠ</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>tearjerker</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53551&amp;course=12136">Lana Štimac</a> - Friday, 19 December 2025, 7:35 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="p1" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;color:#000000;"><span class="s1" style="font-family:UICTFontTextStyleBody;font-size:18.25px;">noun (informal)</span></p>
<p class="p2" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;min-height:23.6px;color:#000000;"></p>
<p class="p1" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;color:#000000;"><span class="s1" style="font-family:UICTFontTextStyleBody;font-size:18.25px;">/ˈtɪəˌdʒɜː.kər/</span></p>
<p class="p2" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;min-height:23.6px;color:#000000;"></p>
<p class="p1" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;color:#000000;"><span class="s2" style="font-family:UICTFontTextStyleEmphasizedBody;font-weight:bold;font-size:18.25px;">a book, film, play etc. that has a sad story intended to make people cry or be sad</span></p>
<p class="p2" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;min-height:23.6px;color:#000000;"></p>
<p class="p1" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;color:#000000;"><span class="s1" style="font-family:UICTFontTextStyleBody;font-size:18.25px;">“Bring a pile of tissues with you when you see that film, it’s a real tear-jerker.”</span></p>
<p class="p1" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;color:#000000;"><span class="s1" style="font-family:UICTFontTextStyleBody;font-size:18.25px;">Ko boš gledal ta film, prinesi s seboj kup robčkov, saj je zelo čustven.</span></p>
<p class="p1" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;color:#000000;"><span class="s1" style="font-family:UICTFontTextStyleBody;font-size:18.25px;"> </span></p>
<p class="p1" style="margin:0px;font-size:18.2px;line-height:normal;color:#000000;"><span class="s1" style="font-family:UICTFontTextStyleBody;font-size:18.25px;">From: </span><a style="font-size:1rem;font-style:inherit;" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/tearjerker">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/tearjerker</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td <table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53416&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Luka Fijavž Vivod" aria-label="Luka Fijavž Vivod" role="img">LF</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>the brunt of something</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53416&amp;course=12136">Luka Fijavž Vivod</a> - Monday, 10 November 2025, 6:14 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/ðə brʌnt əv ˈsʌmθɪŋ/</p>
<p><strong>The worst problems caused by something:</strong></p>
<p><em>He claimed that the middle class would <strong>bear the brunt of</strong> the tax increase.</em></p>
<p><em>Trdil je, da bo srednji razred trpel zadnji udarec zvišanja davkov.</em></p>
<p>From: https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/brunt-of precipitate</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Hana Bric" aria-label="Hana Bric" role="img">HB</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>the tail wagging the dog</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136">Hana Bric</a> - Monday, 22 December 2025, 5:17 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color:#000000;">idiom </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="color:#000000;">/ ðə te</span><span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;">ɪ</span><span style="color:#000000;">l </span><span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;">ˈ</span><span style="color:#000000;">wæ</span><span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;">ɡɪ</span><span style="color:#000000;">ŋ</span><span style="color:#000000;"> ðə d</span><span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;color:#000000;">ɒɡ</span><span style="color:#000000;"> /</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-gb" style="color:#000000;" xml:lang="en-gb">a <a title="situation" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/situation"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">situation</span></a> in which a <a title="large" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/large"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">large</span></a> <a title="group" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/group"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">group</span></a> has to do something to <a title="satisfy" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/satisfy"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">satisfy</span></a> a <a title="small" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/small"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">small</span></a> <a title="group" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/group"><span style="color:#000000;text-decoration:none;">group</span></a></span></strong><strong><span style="color:#000000;"> </span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-us" style="font-size:10.5pt;line-height:107%;font-family:'Segoe UI', sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-us">In today’s creative economy, <span>the tail increasingly wags the dog.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-us" style="font-size:10.5pt;line-height:107%;font-family:'Segoe UI', sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-us">V današnjem ustvarjalnem gospodarstvu se stvari odvijajo v napačnem vrstnem redu. </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-us" style="font-size:10.5pt;line-height:107%;font-family:'Segoe UI', sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-us">From: </span><span lang="en-gb" style="font-size:10.5pt;line-height:107%;font-family:'Segoe UI', sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb"><a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/tail-wagging-the-dog?q=the+tail+wagging+the+dog">THE TAIL WAGGING THE DOG - Cambridge English Dictionary</a></span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: the tail wagging the dog" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91243"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: the tail wagging the dog" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: the tail wagging the dog"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91243&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff605bbb1" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff605bbb1" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff605bbb1">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff605bbb1" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff605bbb1" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff605bbb1" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff605bbb1" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff605bbb1" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff605bbb1"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff605bbb1" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Brina Mohar" aria-label="Brina Mohar" role="img">BM</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>tongue in cheek</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53437&amp;course=12136">Brina Mohar</a> - Monday, 3 November 2025, 11:36 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p><span lang="en-gb" style="font-size:11pt;line-height:107%;font-family:Calibri, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-gb">/ˌtʌŋ ɪnˈtʃiːk/</span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraph" style="text-indent:-18pt;"><span lang="en-gb" style="font-family:Symbol;" xml:lang="en-gb"><span>·<span style="font:7pt 'Times New Roman';">        </span></span></span><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">if you say something tongue in cheek, you intend it to be understood as a joke, although you might appear to be serious (Cambridge Dictionary)</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="en-gb" xml:lang="en-gb">He said he was a huge fan of the president, although I suspect it was <strong>tongue in cheek</strong>. </span><span lang="es" xml:lang="es">(Cambridge Dictionary)</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Rekel je, da je ogromen oboževalec predsednika, čeprav se mi zdi, da se je <strong>šalil</strong>.</p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50433&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Leonela Handanović" aria-label="Leonela Handanović" role="img">LH</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>trigger warning</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50433&amp;course=12136">Leonela Handanović</a> - Sunday, 14 December 2025, 4:08 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><span class="pos"><strong><i>noun</i></strong></span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><span class="gram"><a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/help/codes.html">[<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><span class="gc">C</span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>]</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="region"><strong> UK</strong><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span> <span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><span class="pron">/<span class="ipa">ˈtrɪɡ.ə ˌwɔː.nɪŋ</span></span><span class="pron">/</span></span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span class="region"><strong> US</strong></span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span> <span class="pron">/<span class="ipa">ˈtrɪɡ.ɚ ˌwɔːr.nɪŋ</span></span><span class="pron">/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong>a<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="statement" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/statement">statement</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>at the<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="beginning" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/beginning">beginning</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>of a<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="piece" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/piece">piece</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>of writing, before the<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="start" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/start">start</a>of a<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="film" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/film">film</a>, etc.,<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="warning" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/warning">warning</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="people" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/people">people</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>that they may<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="find" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/find">find</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>the<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="content" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/content">content</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>very<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="upsetting" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/upsetting">upsetting</a>,<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="especially" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/especially">especially</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>if they have<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="experienced" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/experienced">experienced</a><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span>something<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><a title="similar" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/similar">similar</a>:<span class="apple-converted-space"> </span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">ENG: Trigger</span></i><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><span class="eg"><i><a title="warnings" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/warning">warnings</a></i></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><span class="eg"><i>are</i></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><span class="eg"><i><a title="supposed" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/supposed">supposed</a></i></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><span class="eg"><i>to</i></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><span class="eg"><i><a title="protect" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/protect">protect</a></i></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><span class="eg"><i><a title="people" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/people">people</a></i></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><span class="eg"><i>from</i></span><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><span class="eg"><i><a title="post-traumatic" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/post-traumatic-stress-disorder">post-traumatic</a></i></span><i><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl"> flashbacks.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">SLO: Opozorila glede občutljive tematike naj bi ljudi ščitila pred podoživljanjem travmatičnih izkušenj.</span></i></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Nena Horvat" aria-label="Nena Horvat" role="img">NH</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Twinge</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53879&amp;course=12136">Nena Horvat</a> - Saturday, 20 December 2025, 7:14 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>Noun</p>
<p>/twɪndʒ/</p>
<p>A sudden short feeling of physical or mental pain.</p>
<p>I felt a twinge in my knee.</p>
<p>Občutil sem zbadajočo bolečino v kolenu.</p>
<p>Source: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/twinge">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/twinge</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Twinge" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91196"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Twinge" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Twinge"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91196&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff6066e7e" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff6066e7e" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff6066e7e">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff6066e7e" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff6066e7e" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff6066e7e" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff6066e7e" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff6066e7e" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff6066e7e"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff6066e7e" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>U</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Hana Bric" aria-label="Hana Bric" role="img">HB</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>unscathed</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50849&amp;course=12136">Hana Bric</a> - Monday, 15 December 2025, 10:02 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adjective</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">/<span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;">ʌ</span>n<span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;">ˈ</span>ske<span style="font-family:Arial, sans-serif;">ɪ</span>ðd/</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Without <a title="injuries" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/injury"><span style="text-decoration:none;">injuries</span></a> or <a title="damage" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/damage"><span style="text-decoration:none;">damage</span></a> being <a title="caused" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/cause"><span style="text-decoration:none;">caused</span></a>.</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">e.g. Her <a title="husband" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/husband"><span style="text-decoration:none;">husband</span></a> <a title="died" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/die"><span style="text-decoration:none;">died</span></a> in the <a title="accident" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/accident"><span style="text-decoration:none;">accident</span></a> but she, <a title="amazingly" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/amazingly"><span style="text-decoration:none;">amazingly</span></a>, <a title="escaped" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/escaped"><span style="text-decoration:none;">escaped</span></a> unscathed.</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">Translation: Njen mož je v nesreči umrl, a ona jo je začuda odnesla brez poškodb.</p>
<p class="MsoNormal">From: <a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/unscathed">UNSCATHED | English meaning - Cambridge Dictionary</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: unscathed" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=91117"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: unscathed" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: unscathed"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=91117&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff606846b" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff606846b" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff606846b">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff606846b" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff606846b" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff606846b" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff606846b" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff606846b" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff606846b"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff606846b" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<p>to push or move something so that the part that usually touches the ground is not touching the ground any more</p>
<p>She upended the chessboard halfway through the game because she was losing.</p>

<div><table cellspacing="0" class="glossarycategoryheader"><tr><th ><h3>W</h3></th></tr></table></div>
<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50433&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Leonela Handanović" aria-label="Leonela Handanović" role="img">LH</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>walk a fine line (between something and something)</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=50433&amp;course=12136">Leonela Handanović</a> - Thursday, 13 November 2025, 11:47 AM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p class="MsoNormal"><strong><i><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">verbal </span></i></strong><strong><i>idiom</i></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">UK</span></strong> <span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl"> /</span><span class="frnorm">wɔ</span><span class="frnorm">ː</span><span class="frnorm">k</span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><span class="frnorm">ə</span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">'</span><span class="frnorm">fa</span><span class="frnorm">ɪ</span><span class="frnorm">n</span><span class="apple-converted-space"> </span><span class="frnorm">la</span><span class="frnorm">ɪ</span><span class="frnorm">n</span><strong><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">/</span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">US </span></strong>/wɑːk ə <span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">'</span>faɪn laɪn/</p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong>to be in a </strong><a title="difficult" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/difficult"><strong>difficult</strong></a><strong> </strong><a title="situation" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/situation"><strong>situation</strong></a><strong> when you have a </strong><a title="choice" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/choice"><strong>choice</strong></a><strong> between doing one thing and doing another, often where one </strong><a title="action" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/action"><strong>action</strong></a><strong> is </strong><a title="acceptable" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/acceptable"><strong>acceptable </strong></a><strong>and one is not, or the two </strong><a title="actions" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/action"><strong>actions</strong></a><strong> are </strong><a title="opposed" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/opposed"><strong>opposed</strong></a><strong> to each other:</strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i>There are no</i><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><a title="easy" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/easy"><i>easy</i></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><a title="solutions" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/solution"><i>solutions</i></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><i>in</i><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><a title="medicine" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/medicine"><i>medicine</i></a><i>. You're always</i><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><a title="walking" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/walking"><i>walking</i></a><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><i>a</i><span class="apple-converted-space"><i> </i></span><a title="fine" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/fine"><i>fine</i></a><i><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl"> line</span></i><i>.</i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><u><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">TRANSLATION:</span></u><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl"> V medicini ni enostavnih rešitev. Vedno hodiš po tanki črti</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">Cambridge Free English Dictionary and Thesaurus. (2025). Available on: </span><a href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/"><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl">https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/</span></a><span lang="sl" xml:lang="sl"> (obtained 22. 10. 2025).</span></p>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Maj Rengeo" aria-label="Maj Rengeo" role="img">MR</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>walk a tightrope</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53741&amp;course=12136">Maj Rengeo</a> - Monday, 3 November 2025, 6:23 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">/wɔ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ː</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">k ə </span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ˈ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ta</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ɪ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">t</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ˌ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ro</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Arial, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">ʊ</span><span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">p/</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><strong><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">to be in a difficult situation where you must be very careful about what you do or say, because you are trying to satisfy opposing groups.</span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">He is walking a tightrope between the young activists and the more traditional elements within the democracy movement.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><i><span lang="en-si" xml:lang="en-si">Hodi po tanki vrvi med mladimi aktivisti in bolj tradicionalnimi elementi znotraj demokratičnega gibanja.</span></i></p>
<p class="MsoNormal">From: <span lang="en-si" style="font-size:12pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Aptos, sans-serif;" xml:lang="en-si">https://www.collinsdictionary.com/us/dictionary/english/walk-a-tightrope</span></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: walk a tightrope" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90546"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: walk a tightrope" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: walk a tightrope"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90546&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff606d488" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff606d488" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff606d488">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff606d488" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff606d488" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff606d488" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff606d488" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff606d488" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff606d488"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff606d488" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Katarina Dimitrijević" aria-label="Katarina Dimitrijević" role="img">KD</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>Walk on eggshells</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=45613&amp;course=12136">Katarina Dimitrijević</a> - Monday, 1 December 2025, 3:26 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>idiom</p>
<p>/wɔːk ɒn ˈɛɡʃɛlz/</p>
<p><strong>To be very cautious or diplomatic for fear of upsetting someone.</strong></p>
<p>E.g. <span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>Healthy or sick, good days or bad, I felt I was always <strong>walking on eggshells</strong> around him.</em></span></p>
<p>Slovenian translation: <span style="color:#7d9fd3;"><em>Bolna ali zdrava, v dobrih ali slabih trenutkih, vedno sem imela občutek, da moram <strong>hoditi okoli njega kot po jajcih</strong>.</em></span></p>
<p>From: <a href="https://www.collinsdictionary.com/dictionary/english/walk-shorts">https://www.collinsdictionary.com/dictionary/english/walk-shorts</a></p></div></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entrylowersection"><table><tr valign="top"><td class="icons"><span class="commands"><a title="Entry link: Walk on eggshells" class="icon" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/showentry.php?eid=90477"><i class="icon fa fa-link fa-fw "  title="Entry link: Walk on eggshells" role="img" aria-label="Entry link: Walk on eggshells"></i></a></span><div><div class="mdl-left"><a class="showcommentsnonjs" href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/mod/glossary/view.php?id=579823&amp;mode=letter&amp;nonjscomment=1&amp;comment_itemid=90477&amp;comment_context=935286&amp;comment_component=mod_glossary&amp;comment_area=glossary_entry">Show comments</a><a class="comment-link" id="comment-link-6954ff606ea3a" href="#" role="button" aria-expanded="false"><img id="comment-img-6954ff606ea3a" class="icon" src="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/theme/image.php/boost_union_ff/core/1764594199/t/collapsed" alt="Comments" /><span id="comment-link-text-6954ff606ea3a">Comments (<span class="comment-link-count">0</span>)</span></a><div id="comment-ctrl-6954ff606ea3a" class="comment-ctrl"><ul id="comment-list-6954ff606ea3a" class="comment-list"><li class="first"></li></ul><div id="comment-pagination-6954ff606ea3a" class="comment-pagination"></div><div class="comment-area"><div class="db"><label for="dlg-content-6954ff606ea3a" class="sr-only">Comment</label><textarea name="content" rows="2" id="dlg-content-6954ff606ea3a" aria-label="Add a comment..." cols="20"></textarea></div><div class="fd" id="comment-action-6954ff606ea3a"><a id="comment-action-post-6954ff606ea3a" href="#">Save comment</a></div></div><div class="clearer"></div></div></div></div></td></tr></table><hr>

<table class="glossarypost fullwithauthor" cellspacing="0"><tr valign="top"><td class="picture"><a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53747&amp;course=12136" class="d-inline-block aabtn"><span class="userinitials size-35" title="Rebeka Košir" aria-label="Rebeka Košir" role="img">RK</span></a></td><th class="entryheader"><div class="concept"><h4>wary</h4></div><span class="author">by <a href="https://e-ucenje.ff.uni-lj.si/user/view.php?id=53747&amp;course=12136">Rebeka Košir</a> - Sunday, 21 December 2025, 1:13 PM</span></th><td class="entryattachment"></td></tr><tr valign="top"><td class="left">&nbsp;</td><td colspan="2" class="entry"><div class="no-overflow"><p>adjective</p>
<p>/<span class="ipa dipa lpr-2 lpl-1">ˈweə.ri</span>/</p>
<p>not completely trusting or certain about something or someone</p>
<p>I'm a little wary of giving people my address when I don't them very well.</p>
